APIs for E-Filing Service Providers

The EFM APIs for E-Filing Service Providers fall into several broad categories:
  • Configuration
  • Administrative APIs
  • E-Filing APIs
    Details regarding each of these categories are provided below.


    IMPORTANT NOTES

    • The schema folder consists of the ECF 5 WSDLs which define the messages, bindings, and ports. This folder also contains several Tyler specific WSDLs which define additional operations that are not provided by the ECF specification.
    • The service folder contains Tyler implementation specific WSDLs which imports the WSDLs from the schema folder and Tyler extensions where appropriate. These WSDLs define the service and security policy.
    • The WSDLs without the Tyler prefix are our implementation of ECF 5. That is, they only contain bona-fide ECF 5 operations but might include extension elements. Key point: no non-ECF operations are in these WSDLs. The WSDLs with the Tyler prefix are new operations that Tyler has added to cover functionality needs that ECF does not address.
    • The EFM implementation of ECF does not support the xsi:type attribute in XML; instead, the ECF message should explicitly define the common ECF namespace prefix for the element or define it on the element. Use of the xsi:type attribute can cause parsing to fail, which could result in unknown error messages.
    • CodeIDs used in a test or stage environment will be different than the corresponding code's CodeIDs in production.
    • URLs included herein and in the sample files are for demonstration purposes only. The actual URLs vary by market.
    • While most API calls require that a user provide credentials, several APIs do not require user credentials. For such APIs, the EFSP should take measures to prevent abuse (e.g. use of captcha).

    Configuration

    The EFM configuration includes system codes and court specific codes. Some court specific codes pertain only to the initiation of criminal cases. In order to obtain configuration information, first retrieve the system codes, then the court specific codes. You only need to retrieve criminal initiation specific codes if your system serves a prosecutorial agency and therefore would initiate criminal cases.


    Code retrieval requests are via HTTP GET. All code retrieval responses consist of XML that is ZIP compressed. The response schema for all code retrievals is OASIS Genericode. The code field contains the unique identifier for each code row. Some court specific code tables include additional metadata that provides additional information to drive EFM behavior such as whether a particular code value is valid for a given business scenario.

    Access Control
    Access to the code sets is restricted to authorized systems. In order to authenticate your request, include an HTTP header named tyl-api-auth. The content of this header should be the current timestamp, signed via Cryptographic Message Syntax utilizing the same X.509 certificate that you use to sign your SOAP headers, then base64 encoded. Sample .NET and JAVA code is available here

    Caching
    Due to the high degree of configuration within the system, EFSPs should cache the configuration information for quick, on-demand use. Code caches should be refreshed after 1AM of the local timezone in order to pick up configuration changes for the next day. The CodeVersions code table provides checksums of each code table at each court location, which you can use to determine whether you need to refresh your local copy.

    • System Codes
    • Court Specific Codes
    • Criminal Initiation Specific Codes
      Details regarding both types of codes are provided below.

      System Codes

      System codes define system wide behaviors and capabilities of the EFM
        • Court Locations
        • Code Versions
        • Error Codes
        • Country Codes
        • State Codes
        • Filing Status Codes
        • Data Field Configuration Codes
        Details regarding each set of system codes are provided below.

        Court Locations

        This call retrieves a listing of the court locations currently utilizing the EFM. A court location is not necessarily a physical location, but rather, the entire set of court locations is a representation of the state's court organizational structure.

        The code field contains a unique identifier, referred to as the Court Location Identifier (CLI), which is used within various APIs to specify the particular court location for that invocation of the API. The general naming convention of a CLI includes one or two parts:

        • primary - typically a county or a district
        • secondary - an office, division, or court
        If a secondary part exists, the CLI will be of the form primary:secondary. Examples: "tyler" would represent Tyler County, "tyler:dc" would represent the Tyler County District Clerk, or "tyler:dc101" would represent the Tyler County 101st District Court.

        NOTE: The CLIs between STAGE and PROD sites may differ, although this should be rare and is often times transient.

        This call accepts no input parameters. The actual URL will be provided to you by Tyler when you receive access to each site.

        Version3.7
        RequiredCore functionality
        Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/CodeService/codes/location/
        Request Message DefinitionN/A
        Response Message Definitiongenericode
        XML Samples
        DescriptionRequestResponse
        Court LocationsN/ALocations
        Inputs
        FieldDescription
        No Inputs
        Outputs
        FieldDescription
        codeUnique EFM identifier for the code. This field is also known as the Court Location Identifier
        nameTextual description of the code
        initialIndicates whether the location accepts initial/new case filings
        subsequentIndicates whether the location accepts subsequent filings
        disallowcopyingenvelopemultipletimes Indicates whether the location supports the ability to copy an envelope more than once
        allowfilingintononindexedcase Indicates whether the location supports filings into non-indexed cases. Non-indexed cases are cases that exist with the court but are not known to the EFM due to a limited integration with the Clerk's CMS. Non-indexed case filings are submitted similar to a new case filing but the filer also specifies the case number.
        allowablecardtypes A comma delimited list of payment types accepted by the court. Possible values:
        • AMEX
        • CHECKING
        • DISCOVER
        • MASTERCARD
        • VISA
        odysseynodeidIndicates the Odyssey NodeID for a court location that is integrated with Tyler's Odyssey Case Manager
        cmsid Indicates the CMSID - a unique identifier assigned to each instance of a CMS. This is only relevant to court agencies who use the EFM as well as Odyssey Case Manager APIs. This information allows such agencies to use the OdysseyNodeID field in an EFM instance that integrates to multiple Odyssey installations.
        sendservicebeforereviewIndicates whether the EFM will perform e-Service before or after clerk review
        parentnodeidIdentifies the parent court location by providing its code value
        iscountyBoolean to indicate whether this location represents a County
        restrictbankaccountpayment Indicates whether the use of eChecks is restricted to firm users only. When restricted to firm users only, individual users will be unable to submit filings with eChecks and will receive an error 216 - User is restricted from Using eCheck.
        allowmultipleattorneysBoolean to indicate whether this location allows a case party to have more than one attorney
        sendservicecontactremovednotficationsBoolean to indicate whether the EFM will send an email to service contacts when they are detached from a case at this location
        allowmaxfeeamountBoolean to indicate whether this location allows the filer to specify a maximum fee amount to which the reviewer can adjust filings during review
        transferwaivedfeestocmsBoolean to indicate whether the EFM will require a Party Responsible for Fees when a waiver is used at this location
        skippreauthBoolean to indicate whether credit card authorization is disabled
        hasconditionalservicetypes Boolean to indicate whether the available service types are based upon the filing details, thereby overriding the system-wide service contact types
        hasprotectedcasetypes Boolean to indicate that this location has case types that require the EFSP to mask the case category and case type. The specific case types are specified in the hasconditionalservicetypes column
        protectedcasetypes A comma delimited list of case type code ids. For any cases of these case types, the EFSP must mask the case category and case type
        allowzerofeeswithoutfilingparty Boolean to indicate whether the FilingPartyID is required when no fees are due.
        allowserviceoninitial A location specific override to the Data Field Configuration FilingServiceCheckBoxInitial

        • True - Allow service on initial filings at this location
        • False - Do not allow service on initial filings at this location
        • (Empty) - No override in place - use the setting indicated by FilingServiceCheckBoxInitial
        allowaddservicecontactsoninitial Boolean to indicate whether service contacts can be added on initial filings at this location.
        allowredaction Boolean to indicate whether redaction is enabled at this location. Information about integrating with Tyler's document redaction service is available here
        redactionurl The URL for interacting with the redaction service. Information about integrating with Tyler's document redaction service is available here
        redactionviewerurl The URL for launching the redaction viewer/editor. Information about integrating with Tyler's document redaction service is available here
        redactionapiversion The version of the TIS API for courts at which redaction is enabled. Information about integrating with Tyler's document redaction service is available here
        enforceredaction Boolean to indicate whether forced redaction is enabled at this location. Information about integrating with Tyler's document redaction service is available here
        redactiondocumenttype A document type code to indicate the document type (see DocumentTypeCodes) to be included for redacted documents at this location. Information about integrating with Tyler's document redaction service is available here
        defaultdocumentdescription A location specific override to the Data Field Configuration DocumentDescription

        • 1 - Sets the default value to the filing code description (comparable to FilingCode for data field configuration).
        • 2 - Sets the default value to the name of the uploaded file (comparable to FileName for the data field configuration).
        • A NULL value indicates that the field will obey the Data Field Configuration.
        allowwaiveronmail Boolean to indicate whether a waiver account can be used for the mail and certified mail service types at this location.
        showreturnonreject Boolean to indicate whether to use the term "Return" instead of "Reject". If value is True, use the term "Return"
        protectedcasereplacementstring Textual value to use as a replacement for the case category and case type for case types identified by the protectedcasetypes column
        redactionfee Amount that indicates the redaction fee at this location.
        allowwaiveronredaction Boolean to indicate whether or not redaction fees will be waived.
        disallowelectronicserviceonnewcontacts Boolean to indicate that only mail service is allowed for a service contact added to an initial filing.
        allowindividualregistration Boolean to indicate whether or not the system allows an individual to register.
        redactiontargetconfig A comma delimited list of elements to be redacted. Possible values:
        • AccountNumber
        • CreditCard
        • DriversLicense
        • GovernmentID
        • Passport
        • SocialSecurityNumber
        • TaxDocument
        bulkfilingfeeassessorconfiguration Boolean to indicate whether or not the system allows bulk filings
        envelopelevelcommentconfiguration A nullable boolean:
        • Boolean True to indicate an envelope comment is required
        • Boolean False to indicate an envelope comment is not allowed
        • Null to indicate an envelope comment is allowed, but optional
        autoassignsrlservicecontact Boolean to indicate that the system will require self-represented litigants to be a service contact on the case
        When set to true and the filer is a party on the case, the filer must register as a service contact for the case
        autoassignattorneyservicecontact Boolean to indicate that the system will requires attorneys to be a service contact on the case
        When set to true and the GetAttorney API includes an email address (from the state bar feed), the attorney must register as a service contact for the case when filing
        partialwaiverdurationindays The number of days a newly granted standing waiver is valid before expiring
        partialwaivercourtpaymentsystemurl The URL for the court's independent payment system
        partialwaiveravailablewaiverpercentages A list of percentages that maybe be granted for standing waivers



        Code Versions

        This call retrieves a listing of checksums for each code table within each court. The EFSP should use the checksum to determine whether a new version of the court's code table is available. System code tables will appear once whereas location specific code tables will appear once per location.
        Version3.15
        RequiredCore functionality
        Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/CodeService/codes/versions/
        Request Message DefinitionN/A
        Response Message Definitiongenericode
        XML Samples
        DescriptionRequestResponse
        Code VersionsN/ACodeVersions
        Inputs
        FieldDescription
        No Inputs
        Outputs
        FieldDescription
        locationCourt Location Identifier, as defined in Locations code table
        codelistThe .zip filename of the code table
        versionA value that indicates the checksum for this court location's specified code table

        There configuration items fall into two categories:

        • All Filing Types
        • Criminal Initiation

        Configurations: All Filing Types

        Configuration Item Purpose
        AdvancedSearchLocationAllLocations Indicates whether the GetCaseList API can be invoked to perform a case search at the System Location in order to search all court locations. This option will only be available for a site that is backed by a single Courts/Clerks Case Management System.

        • When IsVisible=True, indicates that a case search across all locations is available
        • When IsVisible=False, indicates that a case search across all locations is not available
        • If not defined, defaults to IsVisible=False
        CaseAllowAddNewServiceContacts Provides requirements to indicate whether the filer should be allowed to add a new service contact before submitting the filing:

        • When IsVisible=True, indicates that the functionality should be made available to the filer
        • When IsVisible=False, indicates that the functionality should not be made available to the filer
        • If not defined, defaults to IsVisible=False, IsRequired=False
        CaseInformationCaseSubType Provides requirements regarding the case sub type field:

        • When IsVisible=True, indicates that the field should be made available to the filer
        • When IsVisible=False, indicates that the field should not be made available to the filer
        • When IsRequired=True, indicates that the field is required
        • When IsRequired=False, indicates that the field is optional
        • If not defined, defaults to IsVisible=False, IsRequired=False
        CaseInformationLowerCourt Provides requirements regarding the case information lower court field. This codified field is used for legacy Appellate case filings instead of the textual CaseInformationLowerCourtName field.

        • When IsVisible=True, indicates that the field should be made available to the filer
        • When IsVisible=False, indicates that the field should not be made available to the filer
        • When IsRequired=True, indicates that the field is required
        • When IsRequired=False, indicates that the field is optional
        • If not defined, defaults to IsVisible=False, IsRequired=False
        CaseInformationLowerCourtCaseJudge Provides requirements regarding the lower court judge name field.

        • When IsVisible=True, indicates that the field should be made available to the filer
        • When IsVisible=False, indicates that the field should not be made available to the filer

        • When IsRequired=False, indicates that the field is optional
        • If not defined, defaults to IsVisible=False, IsRequired=False

        • When IsVisible=False, indicates that the field should not be made available to the filer

        • If not defined, defaults to IsVisible=False, IsRequired=False

        DocumentDescription Provides requirements regarding the document description field:

        • When IsVisible=True, indicates that the field should be made available to the filer
        • When IsVisible=False, indicates that the field should not be made available to the filer
        • When IsRequired=True, indicates that the field is required
        • When IsRequired=False, indicates that the field is optional
        • When DefaultValueExpression={{FileName}}, default the document description to document's file name When DefaultValueExpression={{FilingCodeDescription}}, default the document description to the filing code description
        • When IsReadOnly=True, indicates that the field should be made read-only
        • If not defined, defaults to IsVisible=False, IsRequired=False
        • If a RegEx is supplied, it will be used for validating contents of the field
        DocumentType Provides requirements regarding the document type/security field:

        • When IsVisible=False, indicates that the field should not be made available to the filer
        • When IsRequired=True, indicates that the field is required
        • When IsRequired=False, indicates that the field is optional
        • Regular Expression, if defined, will constrain the valid values
        • If not defined, defaults to IsVisible=False, IsRequired=False
        DueDateAvailableForFilers Provides requirements regarding the filing due date field (DocumentInformationCutOffDate):

        • When IsVisible=False, indicates that the field should not be made available to the filer

        • When IsRequired=False, indicates that the field is optional
        • If not defined, defaults to IsVisible=False, IsRequired=False
        FilingEventCaseParties Provides requirements regarding the association of parties to filings:

        • When IsVisible=False, indicates that the party to filing association UI should not be visible to the filer
        • When IsRequired=True, indicates that the filer must indicate associations
        • When IsRequired=False, indicates that the filer may indicate associations
        • If not defined, defaults to IsVisible=True, IsRequired=False
        FilingFilerType Provides requirements regarding the filer type field:

        • When IsVisible=True, indicates that the field should be made available to the filer
        • When IsVisible=False, indicates that the field should not be made available to the filer

        • If not defined, defaults to IsVisible=False, IsRequired=False
        FilingFilingAttorneyView Provides requirements regarding the filing attorney field:

        • When IsVisible=False, indicates that the field should not be made available to firm users
        • When IsRequired=True, indicates that a firm user must provide a filing attorney
        • When IsRequired=False, indicates that a firm user is not required to provide a filing attorney

        FilingFilingComments Provides requirements regarding the filing comments field:

        Court Specific Codes

        Court specific codes define behaviors and field values specific to each court location. Obtain the URL for each code table from the GetPolicy response message.
          • Case Category Codes
          • Case Type Codes
          • Case Sub Type Codes
          • Party Type Codes
          • Filing Codes
          • Filing Component Codes
          • Document Type Codes
          • File Type Codes
          • Optional Services Codes
          • Filer Type Codes
          • Procedure/Remedy Codes
          • Damage Amount Codes
          • Name Suffix Codes
          • Language Codes
          • Cross Reference Codes
          • Disclaimer Requirement Codes
          • Motion Type Codes
          • Service Type Codes
          • Question Codes
          • Answer Codes
          • Refund Reason Codes
          All court specific codes include an EFSPCode column. This column provides a value whereby specialized applications can target a specific entry in the code table. This is configured per arrangement with the courts and not applicable to general purpose EFSPs.

          Additional details regarding each court specific code set are provided below.

          Case Category Codes

          This call retrieves a listing of the valid case category codes for a given court location. Case category codes are similar to ECF case types, therefore this code list includes a field for mapping each case category to an ECF case type. EFSPs use this mapping in order to determine the appropriate ECF Case Type schema for a filing.

          Each case category also includes configuration pertaining to the Procedure/Remedy and Damage Amount code fields, where the available values are:

          • Not Available - the field should not be available to the filer
          • Available - the field should be available to the filer
          • Required - the field should be required of the filer
          Version3.7
          RequiredCore functionality
          Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/CodeService/codes/casecategory/tyler:dc/
          Request Message DefinitionN/A
          Response Message Definitiongenericode
          XML Samples
          DescriptionRequestResponse
          Case Category CodesN/ACaseCategoryCodes
          Inputs
          FieldDescription
          No Inputs
          Outputs
          FieldDescription
          codeUnique EFM identifier for the code
          nameTextual description of the code
          ecfcasetypeThe corresponding ECF Case Type (AppellateCase, CivilCase, etc.)
          procedureremedyinitialIndicates the behavior of the Procedure/Remedy code field for initial filings (Not Available, Available, Required)
          procedureremedysubsequentIndicates the behavior of the Procedure/Remedy code field for subsequent filings (Not Available, Available, Required)
          damageamountinitialIndicates the behavior of the DamageAmount code field for initial filings (Not Available, Available, Required)
          damageamountsubsequentIndicates the behavior of the DamageAmount code field for subsequent filings (Not Available, Available, Required)



          Case Type Codes

          This call retrieves a listing of the valid case type codes for a given court location. Case type codes are more granular than case category codes. Common examples are Divorce, Contract, and Tax. Each case type belongs to a case category. A case type can be configured as to whether the court accepts new filings of that case type, as well as a case initiation fee amount.
          Version3.7
          RequiredCore functionality
          Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/CodeService/codes/casetype/tyler:dc/
          Request Message DefinitionN/A
          Response Message Definitiongenericode
          XML Samples
          DescriptionRequestResponse
          Case Type CodesN/ACaseTypeCodes
          Inputs
          FieldDescription
          No Inputs
          Outputs
          FieldDescription
          codeUnique EFM identifier for the code
          nameTextual description of the code
          casecategoryAssociates the code to a particular case category
          initialA boolean that indicates whether the court accepts new cases of this case type
          feeThe court's fee for initiating a case of this case type
          willfileddateIndicates the behavior of the date field for the filing of a will for this case type (Not Available, Available, Required)
          casestreetaddressIndicates the behavior of the address fields for the filing of this case type (Not Available, Available, Required)



          Case Sub Type Codes

          This call retrieves a listing of the valid case sub type codes for a given court location. Case sub type codes are more granular than case type codes. A case sub type is associated to one or more case types. If a case sub type is associated to more than one case type, it will be repeated in this listing.

          The EFSP should use the casetype field to filter down to values for the current filing. If that list is empty, then the case sub type field should not be shown to the filer.

          Version3.7
          RequiredCore functionality
          Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/CodeService/codes/casesubtype/tyler:dc/
          Request Message DefinitionN/A
          Response Message Definitiongenericode
          XML Samples

          Inputs
          FieldDescription
          No Inputs
          Outputs
          FieldDescription
          codeUnique EFM identifier for the code
          nameTextual description of the code
          casetypeAssociates the code to a particular case type



          Party Type Codes

          This call retrieves a listing of the valid party type codes for a given court location. Party type codes define the types of parties that can be associated to a case. Party types are defined at the court location but may also be defined for specific case types, and some party types are only allowed once on a given case. Fees may be assessed based upon the existence of/number of parties for a case.

          Each party type code also includes configuration pertaining to fields where the available values represent:

          • Not Available - the field should not be available to the filer
          • Available - the field should be available to the filer
          • Required - the field should be required of the filer
          Version3.7
          RequiredCore functionality
          Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/CodeService/codes/partytype/tyler:dc/
          Request Message DefinitionN/A
          Response Message Definitiongenericode
          XML Samples
          DescriptionRequestResponse
          Party Type CodesN/APartyTypeCodes
          Inputs
          FieldDescription
          No Inputs
          Outputs
          FieldDescription
          codeUnique EFM identifier for the code
          nameTextual description of the code
          isavailablefornewpartiesIndicates whether a case can have more than one party with this party type
          casetypeid Indicates an association between the party type and a particular case type.
          isrequired Indicates whether the party type is required in order to initiate a case

          NOTE: This field takes precedence over the isavailablefornewparties field. That is, if casetypeid is non-null, such a party must be provided regardless of the value in the isavailablefornewparties field.

          amount Specifies an amount that will be assessed to the filer when adding a party of this type to the case
          numberofpartiestoignore Specifies the number of parties of this type allowed on the case without incurring a fee
          sendforredaction Boolean to indicate whether the EFSP should send such parties' information to the redaction system for redaction. Only applies for filings where redaction is enabled for the court location
          dateofdeath Indicates the behavior of the date of death field for the party (Not Available, Available, Required)
          displayorder Indicates the display order for required parties on configured case types.



          Filing Codes

          This call retrieves a listing of the valid filing codes for a given court location. In order to determine the valid filing codes for a particular case, the EFSP should perform the following steps:

          1. Union the filing codes that are associated to the case category with the filing codes that are associated to the case type. If that list is empty, then use the filing codes that specify neither a case category nor a case type.
          2. Use the iscourtuseonly field to filter out filing codes that are identified as for court use only
          3. Use the filingtype field to filter out filing codes that are not valid for the current filing

          Each filing code also includes configuration pertaining to several fields where the available values represent:

          • Not Available - the field should not be available to the filer
          • Available - the field should be available to the filer
          • Required - the field should be required of the filer
          Version3.7
          RequiredCore functionality
          Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/CodeService/codes/filing/tyler:dc/
          Request Message DefinitionN/A
          Response Message Definitiongenericode
          XML Samples
          DescriptionRequestResponse
          Filing CodesN/AFilingCodes
          Inputs
          FieldDescription
          No Inputs
          Outputs
          FieldDescription
          codeUnique EFM identifier for the code
          nameTextual description of the code
          feeThe court's fee for a filing of this type
          casecategoryAssociates the code to a particular case category
          casetypeidAssociates the code to a particular case type
          filingtype Indicates whether this filing code is valid for filing a new case (Initial), a filing on an existing case (Subsequent), or both (Both). Under some circumstances, the filing code is no longer valid for use (None)
          iscourtuseonlyIndicates whether the filing code is reserved for court use only
          civilclaimamountIndicates the behavior of the Civil Claim Amount field for filings (Not Available, Available, Required)
          probateestateamountIndicates the behavior of the ProbateEstateAmount field for filings (Not Available, Available, Required)
          amountincontroversyIndicates the behavior of the Ad Damnum field for filings (Not Available, Required)
          useduedateIndicates whether the filing code allows the use of the due date field
          isproposedorder Indicates whether the filing code is configured for use as a proposed order.
          iswaiverrequest Indicates whether the filing code is configured to request a standing waiver from the court.

          The request is specific to the filer and the case. If a waiver request is granted, it will be for a limited duration. The reviewer will receipt the filing to acknowledge that they have received the waiver request. Thereafter, the court will decide whether to grant or deny the waiver, and if granted, whether in part or in full. If granted, the filer will be able to file into that case and automatically receive the percent waived until the waiver expires. Any non-waived fees must still be collected; therefore, the filer must provide a non-waiver payment account when a partial waiver is in effect. Implications for the use of waivers are provided below:

          1. Per Envelope waivers waive all fees for the envelope, including court fees, Tyler fees, and provider fees.
          2. The system will not allow the filer to use a Per Envelope Waiver if the filer has an active Standing Partial Waiver for the case.
          3. Any payment type will be allowed if there is no active standing waiver .
          4. Partial standing waivers waive court fees at the percentage granted by the court.
          5. Partial standing waivers do not waive Tyler fees.
          6. Partial standing waivers do not waive provider fees.
          7. Full standing waivers waive Tyler fees.
          8. Full standing waivers waive provider fees.
          9. If a waiver request is denied the system does not prevent additional waiver requests.



          Filing Component Codes

          This call retrieves a listing of the valid filing component codes for a given court location. Filing components define the types of business documents allowed for the filing -- for instance, lead documents vs. attachments. Filing component codes are associated to specific filing codes, therefore the EFSP must use the filingcodeid field to filter the list to the entries relevant to a given filing. A filing component may be required for a filing type, and may or may not allow multiple occurrences. If no filing component code is defined for a filing type, no documents are allowed.
          Version3.7
          RequiredCore functionality
          Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/CodeService/codes/filingcomponent/tyler:dc/
          Request Message DefinitionN/A
          Response Message Definitiongenericode
          XML Samples
          DescriptionRequestResponse
          Filing Component CodesN/AFilingComponentCodes
          Inputs
          FieldDescription
          No Inputs
          Outputs
          FieldDescription
          codeUnique EFM identifier for the code
          nameTextual description of the code
          filingcodeidAssociates the code to a particular filing code
          requiredIndicates whether or not this filing component is required for the filing
          displayorderAn integer value to represent the order in which to present the filing component. A value will always be present but may be zero, or two rows may have the same value. In either of these cases, the order is irrelevant.
          allowmultipleIndicates whether or not multiple occurrences of this filing component are allowed for the filing
          allowedfiletypesIndicates the types of files that are allowed for this filing component



          Document Type Codes

          This call retrieves a listing of the valid document type codes for a given court location. Document type codes are only applicable if the           DocumentType data field configuration code has IsVisible=true. Document types are associated to specific filing codes and can also be designated for court use only.

          The EFSP should use the filingcodeid field to filter down to values for the current filing. If that list is empty, then use the values where the filingcodeid is empty. Finally, filter out any entries that are marked for court use only.

          Version3.7
          RequiredCore functionality

          isdefaultIndicates that this document type code is the default when configured for a filing code

          Optional Services Codes

          This call retrieves a listing of the valid optional services codes for a given court location. Metadata indicates the filing codes to which each optional service is associated, a fee for the service, and whether an integer multiplier value is required. For instance, certified copies may require the number of copies requested.
          Version3.7
          RequiredCore functionality
          Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/CodeService/codes/optionalservice/tyler:dc/
          Request Message DefinitionN/A
          Response Message Definitiongenericode
          XML Samples
          DescriptionRequestResponse
          Optional Services CodesN/AOptionalServicesCodes
          Inputs
          FieldDescription
          No Inputs
          Outputs
          FieldDescription
          codeUnique EFM identifier for the code
          nameTextual description of the code
          displayorder An integer value to represent the order in which to present the optional services. A value will always be present but may be zero or two rows may have the same value. In either of these cases, the order is irrelevant.
          feeFee associated with this optional service
          filingcodeidFiling code to which the optional service is associated
          multiplierFee multiplier. For instance, a request for 3 certified copies would have a multiplier value of 3
          altfeedescA textual description for a fee that has as calculated value.
          hasfeepromptBoolean to indicate that the filer must provide a fee amount.
          feeprompttextThe text to present to the filer when prompting for the fee amount.
          requiredA boolean to indicate whether the court requires this service.

          Disclaimer Requirement Codes

          A court may require that filers agree to a set of disclaimers before submitting each filing. This call retrieves a listing of such requirements. If such requirements exist, the EFSP must display these disclaimers and require the user to acknowledge each one before allowing the filer to submit.

          NOTE: These disclaimers can include HTML markup. The EFM takes measures to sanitize the content for security purposes but the EFSP should take similar measures as part of a "defense in depth" best practice.

          Version2018.0
          RequiredCore functionality
          Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/CodeService/codes/disclaimerrequirement/tyler:dc
          Request Message DefinitionN/A
          Response Message Definitiongenericode
          XML Samples

          Inputs
          FieldDescription
          No Inputs
          Outputs
          FieldDescription
          codeUnique EFM identifier for the code
          nameTextual description of the code
          listorder An integer value to indicate the order of the disclaimer if there are more than one disclaimer for the court
          requirementtextThe text of the disclaimer to which the filer is agreeing

          Criminal Initiation Specific Codes

            • Arrest Location Codes

            Administrative APIs

            The administrative APIs provide for functionality on behalf of firms and users.
            • Firm Administration APIs
            • User Self-Management
              Access Control
              These APIs require signed SOAP headers to provide system to system authentication. Sample .NET/WCF code is available here.

              The administrative APIs are modeled after ECF, which includes an ErrorCodeText element for returning errors in response to a request. Successful queries return an ErrorCodeText of 0. Failed queries return an appropriate ErrorCodeText value as defined in the court policy.

              Additional details regarding both sets of administrative APIs are provided below.

              Firm Administration APIs

              The EFM Firm Service APIs provide the ability to register and manage users and firms, attorneys, service contacts, and payment accounts.
              • Managing the Firm's Users
              • Managing a Firm
              • Managing Attorneys
              • Managing Service Contacts
              • Using Service Contacts
              • Managing Payment Accounts
              • Global Payment Accounts
                Details regarding each of the firm administration APIs are provided below.

                Managing the Firm's Users

                The following APIs provide the ability to register a new firm and to register and manage additional users.
                  • RegisterUser
                  • AddUserRole
                  • GetUser (Firm Service)
                  • GetUserList
                  • RemoveUser
                  • RemoveUserRole
                  • ResendActivationEmail
                  • ResetUserPassword
                  • UpdateUser (Firm Service)
                  • GetNotificationPreferencesList
                  Details regarding each of the firm user management APIs are provided below.

                  RegisterUser

                  RegisterUser registers a new user within the EFM. The new user may belong to an existing firm, a new firm to be created, or an individual user who is not associated to a firm. All user registrations are subject to an account activation process whereby the EFM sends an activation link to the email address being registered. The associated File & Serve account is not valid for use until the user clicks the verification link.
                  Version3.7
                  RequiredCore functionality
                  Accessible ToIf registration type is FirmAdminNewMember then only firm administrator, otherwise any user. If CSM is enabled, requires the AddNewUsers resource to add users to an existing firm.
                  User CredentialsConditional - If registration type is FirmAdminNewMember then User/PasswordHash required, otherwise an unauthenticated call with no credentials necessary
                  ServiceEFMFirmService
                  Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/EFMFirmService.svc
                  Request Message DefinitionRegistrationRequest
                  Response Message DefinitionRegistrationResponse
                  XML Samples
                  DescriptionRequestResponse
                  New FirmNewFirmRegistrationMessageRegistrationResponseMessage
                  New Firm UserNewFirmUserRegistrationMessageRegistrationResponseMessage
                  New Individual UserNewIndividualUserRegistrationMessageRegistrationResponseMessage
                  Inputs
                  FieldDescription
                  RegistrationTypeThis is the type of user to register. Valid types are:
                  • FirmAdministrator - registers a new firm and its administrator. This value is only valid when creating the firm.
                  • FirmAdminNewMember - registers a new user within an existing firm. This user will be a filer, but a Firm Administrator can promote this user to be a firm administrator via the AddUserRole API.
                  • Individual - registers a new individual user within the system, not associated with a law firm.
                  Refer to CSM when enabled.
                  EmailEmail address for the user to register. The user will use this email address to sign on to the system.
                  FirstNameFirst name of the user to register
                  MiddleNameMiddle name of the user to register.
                  LastNameLast name of the user to register.
                  Password Clear-text password for the user to register. Not required/used for RegistrationType of FirmAdminNewMember. The EFM auto-generates the password and sends it to the user's email address as part of the account activation process. Users should then set their desired password. Password complexity requirements are configured within the EFM. Refer to the GlobalPassword data field configuration code for more information. NOTE: The password field is moot when Okta is enabled. Refer to the Authentication specification for more details.
                  PasswordQuestion NOTE: The password reset question/answer is deprecated in version 3.14; however, this API will continue to accept the fields in order to preserve backward compatibility.

                  Question to use as a password reminder for the registering user. Not required/used for RegistrationType of FirmAdminNewMember

                  PasswordAnswer NOTE: The password reset question/answer is deprecated in version 3.14; however, this API will continue to accept the fields in order to preserve backward compatibility.

                  Answer for the password reminder question. Not required/used for RegistrationType of FirmAdminNewMember

                  StreetAddressLine1Street address of the new firm's address. Required when registering a new firm or individual user account
                  StreetAddressLine2Secondary address apt, unit, etc. of the new firm's address
                  CityCity portion of the new firm's address. Required when registering a new firm or individual user account
                  StateCodeState code of the new firm's address. Required when registering a new firm or individual user account
                  ZipCode Zip code of the new firm's address. US addresses must be of the standard 5 digit or 5-4 digit form. Required when registering a new firm or individual user account
                  CountryCodeCountry code of the new firm's address. Required when registering a new firm or individual user account
                  FirmIDUnique EFM identifier for the firm. Required to register a FirmAdminNewMember
                  FirmNameName of the firm to register. Required to register a FirmAdministrator as it creates a new firm record
                  PhoneNumberPhone number for the new firm. Required when registering a new firm or individual user account
                  FirmIDA new element that distinguishes between a user registering from a firm invitation and a user registering as a new firm.
                  Outputs
                  FieldDescription
                  Error If the EFM is configured to use Okta for authentication and the user already has an active account within Okta, the EFM will return error 960. Please refer to the User Authentication Specification for additional details.
                  UserIDUnique EFM identifier for the new user account
                  PasswordHashResult of the hash function applied to the password
                  ActivationRequiredIndicator as to whether the account has been activated
                  ExpirationDateTimeUTC date/time when the PasswordHash will expire



                  AddUserRole

                  NOTE: This API will return error 1801 when the Composable Security Model is enabled on the site. The GetPolicy API indicates whether CSM is enabled.


                  AddUserRole enables the firm administrator to grant a role to a firm user, where the possible values are Filer and FirmAdmin. The capabilities of each are outlined below.

                  FunctionFilerFirm Admin
                  Search for casesYesYes
                  Submit filingsYesYes
                  Use firm's service contactsYesYes
                  Use firm's payment accountsYesYes
                  Manage his/her account profileYesYes
                  Register new usersNoYes
                  Reset other users' passwordsNoYes
                  Unlock user accounts for firm users locked outNoYes
                  Remove user accounts for firm usersNoYes
                  Designate additional firm administratorsNoYes
                  Create/manage payment accountsNoYes
                  Create/manage attorneysNoYes
                  Create/manage service contactsNoYes
                  View all filings for the firmNoYes

                  Version3.7
                  RequiredCore functionality
                  Accessible ToFirm Administrators Only. If CSM is enabled, this API is deprecated.
                  User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)
                  ServiceEFMFirmService
                  Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/EFMFirmService.svc
                  Request Message DefinitionAddUserRoleRequest
                  Response Message DefinitionBaseResponse
                  XML Samples
                  DescriptionRequestResponse
                  AddUserRoleAddUserRoleMessageBaseResponseMessage
                  AddUserRole - Criminal Filing Filer RoleAddUserRoleMessage-CriminalBaseResponseMessage
                  Inputs
                  FieldDescription
                  UserIDUnique EFM identifier for the firm user
                  Role Role to assign to the user. There are four possible roles:
                  • Filer
                  • FirmAdmin
                  • CriminalFilingFiler - subject to the UserHasCriminalFilingFilerRole data field configuration code
                  • CriminalFilingFirmAdmin - subject to the UserHasCriminalFilingFirmAdminRole data field configuration code
                  A user must have the CriminalFilingFirmAdmin role in order to assign the CriminalFilingFirmAdmin and CriminalFilingFiler roles. Tyler must assign the CriminalFilingFirmAdmin role to the first person in the firm
                  LocationLocation element is only applicable (and required) when assigning the CriminalFilingFiler role
                  Outputs
                  FieldDescription
                  No Outputs



                  GetUser (Firm Service)

                  GetUser enables a firm administrator to retrieve the information for a firm user account.
                  Version3.7
                  RequiredCore functionality
                  Accessible ToFirm Administrators Only. If CSM is enabled, any authenticated user.
                  User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)
                  ServiceEFMFirmService
                  Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/EFMFirmService.svc
                  Request Message DefinitionGetUserRequest
                  Response Message DefinitionGetUserResponse
                  XML Samples
                  DescriptionRequestResponse
                  GetUserGetUserMessageGetUserResponseMessage
                  Inputs
                  FieldDescription
                  UserIDUnique EFM identifier for the user account
                  Outputs
                  FieldDescription
                  UserIDUnique EFM identifier for the user account
                  EmailEmail address for the user
                  FirstNameFirst name of the user
                  MiddleNameMiddle name of the user
                  LastNameLast name of the user
                  LastLoginDateDate and timestamp when the user last logged into the system via the AuthenticateUser API
                  Role NOTE: This element will not be emitted when the Composable Security Model is enabled on the site. The GetPolicy API indicates whether this is enabled.

                  This element repeats as needed to indicate the roles granted to this user. There are two child elements: the role name and the court location for which the user has been granted the role. Valid roles are Filer, FirmAdmin, CriminalFilingFiler, and CriminalFilingFirmAdmin. The location only applies to the CriminalFilingFiler and CriminalFilingFirmAdmin roles. The location element will be empty for all other roles

                  RestrictFilingA read-only boolean indicating whether the user's ability to submit filings has been administratively restricted by Tyler
                  RestrictFilingCommentA read-only description of why the user's ability to submit filing has been restricted
                  IsUndeliverableA read-only boolean indicating whether or not the user's email is deliverable
                  StatusThis element indicates whether a user is Active, Inactive, Deactivated or Suspended.



                  GetUserList

                  GetUserList retrieves a list of the users in the user's firm. If the authenticated user does not have firm administrator privileges, then the returned information is for the current user.
                  Version3.7
                  RequiredCore functionality
                  Accessible ToAny registered user. No different when CSM is enabled.
                  User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)
                  ServiceEFMFirmService

                  No Inputs
                  Outputs
                  FieldDescription
                  UserIDUnique EFM identifier for the user
                  EmailEmail address for the user
                  FirstNameFirst name of the user
                  MiddleNameMiddle name of the user
                  LastNameLast name of the user
                  LastLoginDateDate and timestamp when the user last logged into the system via the AuthenticateUser API
                  Role This element repeats as needed to indicate the role names granted to this user and for which court locations
                  RestrictFilingA read-only boolean indicating whether the user's ability to submit filings has been administratively restricted by Tyler
                  RestrictFilingCommentA read-only description of why the user's ability to submit filing has been restricted
                  IsUndeliverableA read-only boolean indicating whether or not the user's email is deliverable
                  StatusIndicates a user's Status, which can be Active or Suspended.

                  GetNotificationPreferencesList

                  GetNotificationPreferencesList obtains a list of notification emails to which the user may choose to subscribe.
                  Version3.9
                  RequiredConditional functionality, subject to business requirements
                  Accessible ToAny registered user
                  User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)
                  ServiceEFMFirmService
                  Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/EFMFirmService.svc
                  Request Message DefinitionBaseRequest
                  Response Message DefinitionNotificationPreferencesListResponse
                  XML Samples
                  DescriptionRequestResponse
                  GetNotificationPreferencesN/AGetNotificationPreferencesListResponse
                  Inputs
                  FieldDescription
                  No Inputs
                  Outputs
                  FieldDescription
                  ACCEPTEDIndicates whether the EFM will notify when a filing is accepted by the court
                  ACCOUNTLOCKEDIndicates whether the EFM will notify when the user's account has been locked
                  RECEIPTEDIndicates whether the EFM will notify when a filing is receipted by the court. This is not a monetary receipt, but rather, a special purpose form of acceptance of a filing that a jurisdiction may elect to employ
                  REJECTEDIndicates whether the EFM will notify when a filing is rejected, either by the EFM or the court
                  RETURNFORCORRECTIONIndicates whether the EFM will notify when a filing has been returned for correction by the court
                  SERVICEUNDELIVERABLEIndicates whether the EFM will notify when an attempted service cannot be delivered
                  SUBMISSIONFAILEDIndicates whether the EFM will notify when a filing is fails in submission to the EFM
                  SUBMITTEDIndicates whether the EFM will notify when a filing is successfully submitted to the EFM

                    Managing Attorneys

Email address and/or a postal address may be required. Refer to ServiceContactEmailAddress and ServiceContactStreetAddress data field configuration codes for more information.

                        AdministrativeCopy Comma separated list of email addresses to receive an email when this service contact receives electronic service Administrative copies are not sent when service is performed via US Postal Service.                         Using Service Contacts

                          • GetPublicList

                          Outputs

                          DetachServiceContact

                          Managing Payment Accounts

                          Payment Accounts are an EFM construct that facilitates the payment of all fees within File & Serve. These fees include EFSP fees, EFM fees, county fees, and statutory fees. Refer to the GetPaymentAccountTypeList API for obtaining the payment account types available. A waiver account is a request to waive all fees. During clerk review, the clerk determines whether a waiver can be accepted, according to court policy.

                          The following APIs provide the ability to manage the firm's payment accounts.

                            • GetPaymentAccountTypeList
                            • CreatePaymentAccount
                            • GetPaymentAccountList
                            • GetPaymentAccount
                            • RemovePaymentAccount
                            • UpdatePaymentAccount
                            Details regarding the payment account management APIs are provided below.

                            GetPaymentAccountTypeList

                            GetPaymentAccountTypeList retrieves a list of the valid payment account types.
                            Version3.7
                            RequiredCore functionality
                            Accessible ToFirm Administrators Only. If CSM is enabled, requires the ViewPayment resource.
                            User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)
                            ServiceEFMFirmService
                            Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/EFMFirmService.svc
                            Request Message DefinitionBaseRequest
                            Response Message DefinitionPaymentAccountTypeListResponse
                            XML Samples
                            DescriptionRequestResponse
                            GetPaymentAccountTypeListN/APaymentAccountTypeListResponseMessage
                            Inputs
                            FieldDescription
                            No Inputs
                            Outputs
                            FieldDescription
                            CodeIdUnique identifier for the payment account type
                            CodeCode for the payment account type
                            DescriptionDescription of the payment account type



                            CreatePaymentAccount

                            CreatePaymentAccount enables the firm administrator to create a payment account for the firm. To obtain a list of available payment accounts types, use the GetPaymentAccountTypeList API Credit Card and eCheck Accounts These accounts require a filer to obtain a payment token from the Tyler Online Gateway (TOGA) by registering the filer's account information.

                            Waivers These accounts instruct the e-Filing system that the court has waived fees. The review clerk will determine whether the waiver is valid and accept or reject the filing accordingly.

                            Draw Down Accounts These accounts allow filers to e-File with funds that are on file with the clerks office. At present, drawdown accounts are only supported for use with Clerks using Odyssey Case Manager. Filers open and fund a drawdown account directly with the clerk. Such accounts are set up within Odyssey Case Manager for use at one or more court locations, which will result in an account number being provided to the filer. The filer then provides that account number when setting up the account within the EFM, thereby allowing the EFM to validate the account and to obtain the balance and the list of court locations where the account may be used. When a filing is submitted to be paid by drawdown account, the EFM will confirm adequate funds within Odyssey Case Manager. When such filings are accepted by the clerk, the necessary funds will be deducted from the account within Odyssey Case Manager.

                            Cash Accounts These accounts are reserved for use where cash is taken over the counter. By default, anyone can create and use cash accounts, if enabled. It is up to Reviewers to reject filings when they should not be used. Due to this specialty use case, we recommend that EFSPs filter out this payment account type.

                            Version3.7
                            RequiredCore functionality
                            Accessible ToFirm Administrators Only. If CSM is enabled, requires the AddPaymentAccounts resource.
                            User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)
                            ServiceEFMFirmService
                            Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/EFMFirmService.svc
                            Request Message DefinitionCreatePaymentAccountRequest
                            Response Message DefinitionCreatePaymentAccountResponse
                            XML Samples
                            DescriptionRequestResponse
                            CreatePaymentAccount - Credit CardCreatePaymentAccountMessageCreatePaymentAccountResponseMessage
                            CreatePaymentAccount - WaiverCreatePaymentAccountMessage - WaiverCreatePaymentAccountResponseMessage
                            CreatePaymentAccount - eCheckCreatePaymentAccountMessage - eCheckCreatePaymentAccountResponseMessage
                            CreatePaymentAccount - eCheckCreatePaymentAccountMessage - DrawDownCreatePaymentAccountResponseMessage - DrawDown
                            Inputs
                            FieldDescription
                            PaymentAccountTypeCodeA payment account type code as defined by the GetPaymentAccountTypeList API
                            AccountNameName displayed for the payment account
                            AccountToken Payment token identifier. Required for Credit Cards, eChecks, and Draw Downs.

                            For Credit Cards and eChecks, this is the PayorToken field returned by TOGA in response to a filer registering a credit card or eCheck account. For Draw Down accounts, this is the value provided by the court when the draw down account was set up.

                            CardType Type of credit card. This is the first part of the TenderDescription field returned by TOGA in response to a filer registering a credit card or eCheck. Required for PaymentAccountTypeCode value of CC or BankAccount
                            CardLast4 Credit card number's last four digits. This is the last four digits of the TenderDescription field returned by TOGA in response to a filer registering a credit card or eCheck account. Required for PaymentAccountTypeCode value of CC or BankAccount
                            CardMonth Credit card's expiration month. This is the ExpirationMonth field returned by TOGA in response to a filer registering a credit card. Required for PaymentAccountTypeCode value of CC Send a value of 0 for eChecks
                            CardYear Credit card's expiration year. This is the ExpirationYear field returned by TOGA in response to a filer registering a credit card. Required for PaymentAccountTypeCode value of CC. Send a value of 0 for eChecks
                            CardHolderName Credit card's cardholder name. This is the PayorName field returned by TOGA in response to a filer registering a credit card or eCheck account. Required for PaymentAccountTypeCode value of CC or BankAccount
                            CourtIdentifier Applicable only for PaymentAccountTypeCode value of DrawDown. Repeat this element for each court location where a drawdown payment account is to be valid for use. If not provided, the payment account will be available for use at all court locations.

                            NOTE: The CMS ultimately governs where the draw down account can be used.

                            Outputs
                            FieldDescription
                            PaymentAccountID Unique EFM identifier for the payment account
                            PaymentAccountLocation Only applies to DrawDown accounts. Provides balance and minimum balance by court location. May repeat for additional court locations.



                            GetPaymentAccountList

                            GetPaymentAccountList enables a firm member to retrieve a list of the firm's payment accounts.
                            Version3.7
                            RequiredCore functionality
                            Accessible ToAny registered user. If CSM is enabled, requires the ViewPayment resource.
                            User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)

                            Card Type Possible values:
                            • AMEX
                            • CHECKING
                            • DISCOVER
                            • MASTERCARD
                            • VISA
                            This element will not be present for waiver accounts
                            CardLast4 The last 4 digits of the credit card number or bank account number. This element does not apply to waiver accounts
                            CardMonth Two digit expiration month for the credit card. This element does not apply to eCheck and waiver accounts
                            CardYear Four digit expiration year for the credit card. This element does not apply to eCheck and waiver accounts
                            CardHolderName The name on the credit card or bank account, as obtained from TOGA. This element does not apply to waiver accounts

                            Global Payment Accounts

                            The following APIs provide the EFSP the ability to manage global payment accounts. The purpose of a global payment account is to extend credit to the EFSP's firms.

                            While a regular payment account is specific to a particular firm, a global payment account is specific only to a particular EFSP - it is not associated with a particular firm. Therefore, the EFSP can use a global payment account to register a credit card or bank account that is owned by the EFSP, then allow firms to use that global payment account.

                            The EFM allows the global payment account to be used for any filings submitted from the EFSP who owns the account. The EFSP is responsible for determining which firms are allowed to submit filings with the global payment account. The EFSP is also responsible for invoicing/billing/collecting from the firms for use of the payment account.

                              • CreateGlobalPaymentAccount
                              • GetGlobalPaymentAccountList
                              • GetGlobalPaymentAccount
                              • RemoveGlobalPaymentAccount
                              • UpdateGlobalPaymentAccount
                              Details regarding the global payment account management APIs are provided below.

                              CreateGlobalPaymentAccount

                              CreateGlobalPaymentAccount enables an EFSP to create a global payment account. The message definitions for this API are identical to CreatePaymentAccount.
                              Version3.7
                              RequiredConditional functionality, subject to business requirements
                              Accessible ToEFSP initiates this call with no user context
                              User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)
                              ServiceEFMFirmService
                              Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/EFMFirmService.svc
                              Request Message DefinitionCreatePaymentAccountRequest
                              Response Message DefinitionCreatePaymentAccountResponse
                              XML Samples
                              DescriptionRequestResponse
                              CreatePaymentAccount - Credit CardCreatePaymentAccountMessageCreatePaymentAccountResponseMessage
                              CreatePaymentAccount - WaiverCreatePaymentAccountMessage - WaiverCreatePaymentAccountResponseMessage
                              CreatePaymentAccount - eCheckCreatePaymentAccountMessage - eCheckCreatePaymentAccountResponseMessage
                              Inputs
                              FieldDescription
                              *** Refer to the CreatePaymentAccount API ***
                              Outputs
                              FieldDescription
                              *** Refer to the CreatePaymentAccount API ***

                              GetGlobalPaymentAccount

                              User Self-Management

                              The EFM User Service allows an existing user to authenticate with the system as well as to manage his/her account.
                                • AuthenticateUser
                                • ChangePassword
                                • GetPasswordQuestion
                                • ResetPassword
                                • GetUser (User Service)
                                • UpdateUser (User Service)
                                • GetNotificationPreferences
                                • UpdateNotificationPreferences
                                • SelfResendActivationEmail
                                Details regarding each user self-management API are provided below.

                                AuthenticateUser

                                AuthenticateUser authenticates a user's credentials within the EFM. The EFM will return a unique value that the EFSP should then use in lieu of the user's password for subsequent interactions with the EFM on behalf of the user. This eliminates the need for the EFSP to store a user's human readable password.

                                Five failed attempts to log in within a ten-minute timeframe triggers a lock on the associated account. Once locked, an account can be unlocked via either of these actions:

                                • Firm administrator unlocks the account. Refer to the ResetUserPassword API.
                                • User initiates the password reset operation. Refer to the ResetPassword API.

                                NOTE: You only need to call this API when seeking verification of user provided credentials in order to obtain a PasswordHash from the EFM. Once successful, you need not call this API again until either the user attempts a subsequent sign on, or the existing PasswordHash expires (error code -4)

                                Version3.7
                                RequiredCore functionality
                                Accessible ToAny registered user
                                User CredentialsUnauthenticated call - No credentials necessary
                                ServiceEFMUserService
                                Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/EFMUserService.svc
                                Request Message DefinitionAuthenticateRequest
                                Response Message DefinitionAuthenticateResponse
                                XML Samples
                                DescriptionRequestResponse
                                AuthenticateUserAuthenticateRequestMessageAuthenticateResponseMessage
                                Inputs
                                FieldDescription
                                EmailEmail address of the user account
                                Password Password for the account

                                NOTE: When Okta is enabled for authentication, this element should contain the JWT returned from Okta instead of a user provided password.
                                Outputs
                                FieldDescription
                                UserIDUnique EFM identifier for the user account
                                EmailEmail address of the user account
                                FirstNameFirst name of the user
                                LastNameLast name of the user
                                PasswordHash Unique value assigned to the user by the EFM for subsequent interactions with the EFM. While the value is actually a GUID, the concept is similar to a password hash for the user
                                ExpirationDateTimeUTC date/time when the PasswordHash will expire
