                                E-Filing APIs

                                E-Filing APIs are implemented according to the ECF Major Design Elements (MDEs) and Tyler extensions of the ECF MDEs.
                                • Court Policy MDE Service
                                • Filing Review MDE Service
                                • Filing Assembly MDE Service
                                • Court Record MDE Service
                                • Service MDE Service
                                • Court Scheduling MDE Service
                                • Tyler Extension: Filing Review MDE Service
                                • Tyler Extension: Filing Assembly MDE Service
                                • Tyler Extension: Court Record MDE Service
                                • Tyler Extension: Court Scheduling MDE Service
                                  Access Control
                                  These APIs require signed SOAP headers to provide system to system authentication. Sample .NET/WCF code is available here.

                                  ECF includes an ErrorCodeText element for returning errors in response to a request. Successful queries return an ErrorCodeText of 0. Failed queries return an appropriate ErrorCodeText value as defined in the court policy.

                                  Additional details for each API are provided below.

                                  Court Policy MDE Service

                                  The Court Policy MDE Service includes a single API that enables the EFSP to query court policy.
                                    • GetPolicy
                                    Details regarding this API are provided below.

                                    GetPolicy

                                    GetPolicy retrieves the machine-readable court policy, which contains a list of base URLs whereby court specific codes can be obtained, as well as EFM behavioral characteristics.
                                    Version2022.0
                                    RequiredCore functionality
                                    Accessible ToAny registered user
                                    User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)
                                    ServiceCourtPolicyMDEService
                                    Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/v5/courtpolicyservice.svc
                                    Request Message Definitionpolicyrequest
                                    Response Message Definitionpolicyresponse
                                    XML Samples
                                    DescriptionRequestResponse
                                    GetPolicytyler-policyrequesttyler-policyresponse
                                    Inputs
                                    FieldDescription
                                    Court Location The OrganizationIdentification/IdentificationID element must contain a valid Court Location Identifier, which identifies the court location for which the court policy is desired. The valid values are defined by configuration. Refer to Court Locations codes.
                                    /policyrequest:GetPolicyRequestMessage/j:CaseCourt/nc:OrganizationIdentification/nc:IdentificationID
                                    Outputs
                                    FieldDescription
                                    Code Fields Defines the code fields used within the EFM. ECFElementNameText specifies the element name within the ECF messages where the codified field will be stored. ExtensionLocationURI contains the URL whereby the valid list of code values may be obtained from the EFM. Please refer to the Configuration section of this API Reference Guide for more information about each code table.
                                    /policyresponse:GetPolicyResponseMessage/policyresponse:RuntimePolicy/policyresponse:CodeListExtension
                                    Maximum Document SizeDefines the maximum size for any single document that may be submitted with a filing. The size is enforced upon the file in its native form (e.g. PDF, not base64 encoded)
                                    /policyresponse:GetPolicyResponseMessage/policyresponse:DevelopmentPolicy/policyresponse:MaximumAllowedAttachmentSize
                                    Maximum Message SizeDefines the maximum total size for all documents that may be submitted with an envelope. The size is enforced upon the file in its native form (e.g. PDF, not base64 encoded)
                                    /policyresponse:GetPolicyResponseMessage/policyresponse:DevelopmentPolicy/policyresponse:MaximumAllowedMessageSize
                                    SupportedCaseCategoriesSpecifies with ECF case types are supported at this court location
                                    /policyresponse:GetPolicyResponseMessage/policyresponse:DevelopmentPolicy/policyresponse:SupportedCaseCategories
                                    Schema Extensions Specifies Tyler's extensions to the ECF schemas
                                    /policyresponse:GetPolicyResponseMessage/policyresponse:DevelopmentPolicy/policyresponse:SchemaExtension
                                    Session Timeouts This pair of values defines the expiration model for user password GUIDs. TimeoutMinutes defines the number of minutes before a user password GUID will be subject to timeout. TimeoutResetHour defines the UTC time of day when GUID timeouts will take effect.

                                    Example:
                                    TimeoutMinutes = 1440 (24 hours)
                                    TimeoutResetHour = 02:00:00Z

                                    - A password GUID issued at 01:59:00Z will be valid for 1441 minutes (24 hours and 1 minute).
                                    - A password GUID issued at 02:01:00Z will be valid for 2879 minutes (47 hours and 59 minutes).

                                    NOTE: This configuration drives the expiration but the EFM emits the actual expiration for each GUID upon issuance.
                                    /policyresponse:GetPolicyResponseMessage/tylercommon:GetPolicyResponseMessageAugmentation/tylercommon:TimeoutMinutes
                                    /policyresponse:GetPolicyResponseMessage/tylercommon:GetPolicyResponseMessageAugmentation/tylercommon:TimeoutResetHour

                                    Court URL A URL that leads to the court's website or e-Filing information.
                                    /policyresponse:GetPolicyResponseMessage/common:GetPolicyResponseMessageAugmentation/common:LocationSpecificURI
                                    UseComposableSecurity A boolean that indicates whether the Composable Security Model is in use. If true, the Composable Security Model micro-service is in use. If false, the EFM is responsible for user access management (legacy model).
                                    /policyresponse:GetPolicyResponseMessage/common:GetPolicyResponseMessageAugmentation/common:UseComposableSecurity
                                    ComposableSecurityURI Provides the endpoint for the Composable Security Model micro-service.
                                    /policyresponse:GetPolicyResponseMessage/common:GetPolicyResponseMessageAugmentation/common:ComposableSecurityURI
                                    ComposableSecurityTenant For use with Tyler's multi-tenant micro-services, this provides the tenant ID corresponding to this EFM site
                                    /policyresponse:GetPolicyResponseMessage/common:GetPolicyResponseMessageAugmentation/common:ComposableSecurityTenant/nc:IdentificationID
                                    ComposableSecurityDefaultRole Provides a role which the EFM will automatically assign to a user who registers with RegistrationType of FirmAdministrator or Individual. This element will repeat if more than one role is to be assigned.

                                    The EFM does not automatically assign any roles for users registered with RegistrationType of FirmAdminNewMember.
                                    IdentificationID provides the unique roleKey
                                    /policyresponse:GetPolicyResponseMessage/common:GetPolicyResponseMessageAugmentation/common:ComposableSecurityDefaultRole/nc:IdentificationID

                                    UseOktaAuthentication A boolean that indicates whether Okta integration is in use. If true, Okta is used for user authentication and account management. If false, the EFM is responsible for user authentication and account management (legacy model).
                                    /policyresponse:GetPolicyResponseMessage/common:GetPolicyResponseMessageAugmentation/common:UseOktaAuthentication
                                    OktaAuthenticationURI Provides the Okta endpoint
                                    /policyresponse:GetPolicyResponseMessage/common:GetPolicyResponseMessageAugmentation/common:OktaAuthenticationURI
                                    BlackoutStatus When a court location is in a blackout, the following will be returned:
                                    • ReasonDescriptionText - the reason entered for the blackout
                                    • BlackoutDate - the Start and End dates

                                    /policyresponse:GetPolicyResponseMessage/common:GetPolicyResponseMessageAugmentation



                                    Filing Review MDE Service

                                    The Filing Review MDE Service contains APIs that enable the EFSP to calculate fees for potential filings, submit and cancel filings, and query the status of filings.
                                      • GetFeesCalculation
                                      • ReviewFiling
                                      • ReviewFiling: Appellate Case Augmentation
                                      • ReviewFiling: Criminal Case Augmentation
                                      • ReviewFiling: Citation Case Augmentation
                                      • GetFilingList
                                      • GetFilingStatus
                                      • CancelFiling
                                      Details regarding the Filing Review MDE APIs are provided below.

                                      GetFeesCalculation

                                      GetFeesCalculation submits an envelope for the purpose of calculating fees. The envelope's filings are not actually filed with the Court. There is no need to include the document binaries in the message. The calculated fees include statutory court costs and fees, along with applicable e-filing fees and payment processing convenience fees. The request message is a FilingMessage. Please refer to ReviewFiling for more details about the FilingMessage.
                                      Version2022.0
                                      RequiredCore functionality
                                      Accessible ToAny registered user. If CSM is enabled, requires the SubmitEnvelopes resource.
                                      User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)
                                      ServiceFilingReviewMDEService
                                      Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/v5/filingreviewservice.svc

                                      Page Count A count of the number of pages in the document. This value is used for calculating the filing fee in some jurisdictions. The EFSP must pass this value since document binaries are not sent to the EFM.

                                      NOTE: This field is not necessary for ReviewFiling as the EFM will count the pages in the document binaries

                                      /feesrequest:GetFeesCalculationRequestMessage/filing:FilingMessage/filing:FilingLeadDocument/ecf:DocumentAugmentation/ecf:DocumentRendition/nc:Attachment/common:AttachmentAugmentation/common:PageCount

                                      Outputs
                                      FieldDescription
                                      Court Location The court location identifier
                                      /feesresponse:GetFeesCalculationResponseMessage/j:CaseCourt/nc:OrganizationIdentification/nc:IdentificationID
                                      Fees An AllowanceCharge structure represents a fee. Repeats for each fee applicable to the filing. Some fees do not apply in all markets. AllowanceChargeReason provides a description of the fee. Amount provides the fee amount. Some fees include additional elements to provide more information.
                                      /feesresponse:GetFeesCalculationResponseMessage/cac:AllowanceCharge/cbc:AllowanceChargeReason
                                      /feesresponse:GetFeesCalculationResponseMessage/cac:AllowanceCharge/cbc:Amount



                                      The AllowanceChargeReason values are listed below, along with any additional context.

                                      Case Initiation FeeCourt fees associated with case initiation
                                      Party Fee Court fees associated with the addition of a party. ID providces the Party type code
                                      /feesresponse:GetFeesCalculationResponseMessage/cac:AllowanceCharge/cbc:ID
                                      Filing Fee Filing fees associated with the filing. ID provides the Filing code
                                      /feesresponse:GetFeesCalculationResposnseMessage/cac:AllowanceCharge/cbc:ID
                                      Optional Service Fee Court fees for any optional services selected by the filer ID provides the Filing code for the associated services. MultiplierFactorNumeric provides the fee multiplier. PerUnitAmount provides the amount per instance of the fee.
                                      /feesresponse:GetFeesCalculationResponseMessage/cac:AllowanceCharge/cbc:ID
                                      /feesresponse:GetFeesCalculationResponseMessage/cac:AllowanceCharge/cbc:MultiplierFactorNumeric
                                      /feesresponse:GetFeesCalculationResponseMessage/cac:AllowanceCharge/cbc:PerUnitAmount
                                      Mail Service Fee A mail service fee associated with a filing. This occurs when the service type is mail or certified mail.
                                      Total Service FeesEFM Fees
                                      Total Service Tax FeesTax on the EFM fees
                                      Redaction FeeRedaction fee associated with a document
                                      Total Redaction FeesTotal redaction fees associated with a filing
                                      Convenience FeePayment processing fees
                                      Total Provider Service FeesEFSP Fees
                                      Total Provider Tax FeesTax on the EFSP fees
                                      Total Court Service FeesThe county cost recovery fee for e-filing
                                      Total Mail Service FeesTotal of all mail service fees
                                      Total Fees The total amount of fees calculated
                                      /feesresponse:GetFeesCalculationResponseMessage/feesresponse:FeesCalculationAmount/nc:Amount



                                      ReviewFiling

                                      ReviewFiling submits a filing to the court. A filing can be an initial filing (filing a new case) or a subsequent filing (filing into an existing case). Before assembling a subsequent filing, the EFSP system should always call                                       GetCaseList and GetCase first in order to load the latest information for the case. A subsequent filing can be used to add parties to a case, or to add attorneys to existing parties; however, it cannot be used to edit existing party information or to change existing attorney assignments, including pro se.

                                      The ReviewFiling request is a compound message that includes both a FilingMessage and a PaymentMessage. The FilingMessage may be repeated to represent more than one filing in an envelope, as long as they pertain to the same court case. The PaymentMessage represents the method of payment for the envelope, and should include an EFSP fee amount and a corresponding EFSP sales tax amount if such fees are to be charged. The EFSP is responsible for calculating the EFSP sales tax amount.

                                      For courts that lack a full integration with the EFM, cases that did not originate through the e-filing system will not initially be known to the EFM. These are known as non-indexed cases. However, a filer can still electronically file into a non-indexed case. Refer to Locations for relevant attribution. Once such a filing has been accepted by the court, the case will become indexed and thus, retrievable via the EFM's GetCaseList and GetCase mechanisms.

                                      The system includes several fields that are intended for batch filing purposes. This functionality has dependencies beyond the EFM, therefore this capability is reserved to limited jurisdictions that have contracted for this additional capability.

                                      This section includes elements of the filing message that apply regardless of case type. See also

                                      • ReviewFiling: Appellate Case Augmentation
                                      • ReviewFiling: Citation Case Augmentation
                                      • ReviewFiling: Criminal Case Augmentation.

                                      NOTE: Currently, the EFM only supports Citations in conjunction with a corresponding Criminal case.

                                      The EFM asynchronously invokes the NotifyFilingReviewComplete API for each filing as a callback to the EFSP to communicate the outcome of each filing.

                                      Version2022.0
                                      RequiredCore functionality
                                      Accessible ToAny registered user. If CSM is enabled, requires the SubmitEnvelopes resource.
                                      User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)
                                      ServiceFilingReviewMDEService
                                      Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/v5/filingreviewservice.svc
                                      Request Message Definitionfiling
                                      payment
                                      appellate
                                      bankruptcy
                                      citation
                                      civil
                                      criminal
                                      domestic
                                      juvenile
                                      common
                                      taxdelinquency
                                      Response Message Definitioncbrn
                                      XML Samples
                                      DescriptionRequestResponse
                                      Filing Message for Appellate Case Initiationtyler-initial-appellate-filingmessageN/A

                                      FieldDescription
                                      Service Contact Indicates that a service contact should receive service. The ServiceRecipient's ID attribute provides an identifier that can be used to reference the service contact elsewhere within the message. The ServiceContactID element provides the EFM identifier for the service contact. The CaseRepresentedParty element is used to associate the service contact to a party on a case. If not associated to a particular party then the service contact is attached to the case. This ServiceRecipient structure is repeated for each service contact to receive service.

                                      The ServiceTypeCode eleement identifies the Service Type code. If the service method is not specified it will default to e-service. The service contact record must have the information necessary to complete the type of service requested, otherwise the EFM will reject the submission.
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/ecf:ElectronicServiceInformation/tylercommon:ElectronicServiceAugmentation/tylercommon:ServiceRecipient/@structures:id
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/ecf:ElectronicServiceInformation/tylercommon:ElectronicServiceAugmentation/tylercommon:ServiceRecipient/tylercommon:ServiceContactID/nc:IdentificationID
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/ecf:ElectronicServiceInformation/tylercommon:ElectronicServiceAugmentation/tylercommon:ServiceRecipient/ecf:CaseRepresentedParty
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/ecf:ElectronicServiceInformation/tylercommon:ElectronicServiceAugmentation/tylercommon:ServiceRecipient/tylercommon:ServiceContactID/tylercommon:ServiceTypeCode

                                      Additional Document Represents any additional documents assocated to a filing. Use PrimaryDocument to reference to associate the document to the appropriate filing May be repeated to represent multiple documents but is subject to court policy document and total envelope size constraints. Refer to the GetPolicy API for more information.
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/filing:FilingConnectedDocument

                                      Filing Action Determines the action for the filing (EFile, EFileAndServe, Serve). All three actions are valid for the ReviewFiling API. The ServeFiling API assumes a FilingAction of Serve, therefore any other action will be ignored.

                                      If no FilingAction is provided, the original default behavior applies. That is:

                                      • ReviewFiling API without service contacts - EFile
                                      • ReviewFiling API with service contacts - EFileAndServe
                                      • ServeFiling API - Serve
                                      NOTE: The service contacts are still specified at the envelope level, so any filings to serve will be served to the same service contacts
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/filing:FilingLeadDocument/tylercommon:DocumentAugmentation/tylercommon:FilingAction
                                      Party to Filing Association The business scenarios for this capability vary by jurisdiction. Represents a relationship between a case party to a specific filing in the envelope. This structure can be repeated as necessary to reflect multiple relationships. This field is governed by the FilingEventCaseParties data field configuration code
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/filing:FilingLeadDocument/tylercommon:DocumentAugmentation/tylercommon:FilingAssociation/tylercommon:PartyReference
                                      Optional Service IdentificationID must contain a valid OptionalServices code

                                      MultiplierAmount provides a fee multiplier for the optional service. A value must be provided if the optional services code is configured to require a multiplier. Refer to Optional Services Codes for more details.

                                      Amount contains a filer provided fee amount. A value must be provided if the optional services code is configured to use a fee prompt. Refer to Optional Services Codes for more details.

                                      Batch Filing Batch filing is available in limited jurisdictions. Batch filing requires additional coordination between Tyler and the clerks
                                      • BatchID is a unique batch identifier to be provided by the EFSP. A GUID is recommended for this value, and may contain only alphabet (A-Z) characters, numbers (0-9), and the dash (-) character.
                                      • BatchName provides the title of the batch.
                                      • BatchSize is an integer representing the number of envelopes that will be submitted in the batch. This value should be constant for each envelope within the batch.
                                      • BatchSequence is an integer that represents the Nth envelope within the named batch. Must be a positive, non-zero integer that is unique within the batch and less than or equal to the batch size
                                      • BatchType os a batch code to identify the type of batch specified.
                                      • Group Identifier is for grouping of case participants
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/tylercommon:FilingMessageAugmentation/tylercommon:Batch/tylercommon:BatchIdentification/nc:IdentificationID
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/tylercommon:FilingMessageAugmentation/tylercommon:Batch/tylercommon:BatchName
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/tylercommon:FilingMessageAugmentation/tylercommon:Batch/tylercommon:BatchSize
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/tylercommon:FilingMessageAugmentation/tylercommon:Batch/tylercommon:BatchSequence
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/tylercommon:FilingMessageAugmentation/tylercommon:Batch/tylercommon:BatchType

                                      /filing:FilingMessage/j:CaseCourt/nc:OrganizationIdentification/nc:IdentificationID
                                      Attorney Attorneys can be either:
                                      • Case Party Attorneys - an instance record of an attorney representing a party on the case
                                      • Filing Attorneys - an attorney who is filing but is not representing a party on the case
                                      IdentificationID provides the EFM identifier for an attorney within the filer's firm. Refer to the Attorney Management APIs for more information.
                                      CaseRepresentedParty associates the attorney to the party being represented and can be repeated if representing multiple parties.

                                      The system can support multiple Case Party Attorney records for each CaseParty. This capability is enabled by default but can be disabled per court location. Refer to Locations for relevant attribution.

                                      One such Case Party Attorney is designated as the lead attorney via the IsLead element. If multiple Case Party Attorneys are specified for a Case Party, one and only one must be designated as the lead. A case party's lead attorney cannot be changed via e-filing. For backward compatibility, if there is only one Case Party Attorney for a given Case Party, the EFM will default that record to be the lead.

                                      Case Party This structure defines a party that is associated to the case.

                                      A subsequent filing need not include a case party existing case parties. Rather, a case party is only necessary for a party that is being added to the case or if the participant is relevant to some aspect of the filing (e.g. to be designated as the filing party, or to be associated to the filing via FilingAssociation)

                                      Case Sub Type A valid Case Sub Type code if the case type allows for a case sub type.
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/nc:Case/tylercommon:CaseAugmentation/tylercommon:CaseSubTypeCode
                                      Person Associations Reserved for Tax Delinquency cases, the PersonAssociation structure provides the ability to relate case participants together. The structure may be repeated as necessary to reflect one or more such associations. This data is not incorporated into Odyssey File & Serve nor Odyssey Case Manager - it is merely passed to the 3rd party Clerk CMS. The values are free text.
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/nc:Case/ecf:CaseAugmentation/nc:PersonAssociation/nc:Person
                                      Case Abstractor & Fees Reserved for Tax Delinquency cases, the CaseAbstractor structure provides the ability to the name of an abstractor and associated fees. The structure may be repeated as necessary to reflect one or more aliases for each case participant. This data is not incorporated into Odyssey File & Serve nor Odyssey Case Manager - it is merely passed to the 3rd party Clerk CMS. The values are free text.
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/nc:Case/tylertax:CaseAugmentation/tylertax:CaseAbstractor/tylertax:Abstractor/nc:EntityOrganization/nc:OrganizationName
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/nc:Case/tylertax:CaseAugmentation/tylertax:CaseAbstractor/tylertax:Fees/nc:Amount
                                      Tax Service of Party Reserved for Tax Delinquency cases, the PartyService structure provides the ability to specify a service type and delivery method. The structure may be repeated as necessary to reflect this information for each case participant. This data is not incorporated into Odyssey File & Serve nor Odyssey Case Manager - it is merely passed to the 3rd party Clerk CMS. The values are free text.
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/nc:Case/tylertax:CaseAugmentation/tylertax:PartyService/tylercommon:PartyReference

                                      /filing:FilingMessage/nc:Case/tylertax:CaseAugmentation/tylertax:PartyService/tylertax:DeliveryMethodCode
                                      Property Account Number Reserved for Tax Delinquency cases, the PropertyAccountNumber structure provides the ability to pass account numbers to the court. The structure may be repeated as necessary to reflect one or more account numbers for the case. This data is not incorporated into Odyssey File & Serve nor Odyssey Case Manager - it is merely passed to the 3rd party Clerk CMS. The values are free text.

                                      Will Filed Date The date for the filing of the will.
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/nc:Case/tylercommon:CaseAugmentation/tylercommon:WillFiledDate
                                      Case Address Physical address associated with the case. The address is configurable by the case type to be required, optional, or not supported. Note that partial addresses are not allowed. If any information is provided, then street, city, state, county, and zip are all required. For example, you cannot provide a state name without providing street information, zip code, and county. Values are free text except for the state codes. US is the only country code supported. Only one address is allowed per case.
                                      /filing:FilingMessage/nc:Case/tylercommon:CaseAugmentation/tylercommon:CaseAddress/tylercommon:AddressAugmentation/tylercommon:AddressSecondaryLine

                                      Error In all TEST EFM environments certain dollar amounts will trigger errors within the Chase Paymentech TEST system. Payment processing consists of two credit card/bank account transactions: a primary transaction for monies due to the court and a secondary transaction for any other monies due. While either the primary or secondary amount can technically trigger the errors, in practice only the primary amount is large enough to do so. Trigger amounts are provided in the following spreadsheet: Chase Test System - Trigger Amounts.xlsx
                                      EFM Identifiers The DocumentIdentification structure is repeated as necessary to return the EFM's unique identifiers appropriate for the filing that was submitted. The IdentificationID element provides the unique EFM identifier and the IdentificationCategoryDescriptionText provides the type of identifier.
                                      • CaseID - An identifier for the case. Only applicable for initial filings
                                      • EnvelopeID - A unique integer based envelope number assigned by the EFM. This envelope number should be provided to the filer as it provides a means of identifying their submission. This identifier is also visible to the clerk reviewers.
                                      • FilingID - Repeated for each filing in the envelope, in reverse order.

                                      /cbrn:MessageStatus/ecf:MessageStatusAugmentation/nc:DocumentIdentification/nc:IdentificationID
                                      /cbrn:MessageStatus/ecf:MessageStatusAugmentation/nc:DocumentIdentification/nc:IdentificationCategoryDescriptionText
                                      DocumentReceivedDate UTC Date/Time stamp of when the envelope was received by the EFM.
                                      /cbrn:MessageStatus/cbrn:SystemEventDateTime
                                      BulkID If the envelope is part of a Bulk Filing, a BulkID is returned.
                                      /cbrn:MessageStatus/ecf:MessageStatusAugmentation
                                      BlackoutStatus When a court location is in a blackout, the following will be returned:
                                      • ReasonDescriptionText - the reason entered for the blackout
                                      • BlackoutDate - the Start and End dates

                                      ReviewFiling: Criminal Case Augmentation

                                      This section outlines the items within the Criminal Case Augmention for case initiation. While any of the elements below may be used for a 3rd party CMS, some fields are valid only for specifically configured court locations. Please refer to the                                       ReviewFiling API for additional information that pertains to the use of ReviewFiling in general.

                                      For criminal case initiations note that the EFM requires one and only one defendant party type and at least one offense charged to that defendant. The offense requires:

                                      • Statute code
                                      • Charge description
                                      • Degree
                                      • Offense date or date range

                                      IMPORTANT: The CMS may have additional requirements for initiating criminal cases, either generally or specifically for your jurisdiction's unique requirements.

                                      GetFilingList

                                      GetFilingList retrieves a list of filings matching several criteria including the filer identifier and filed date within a certain time range. If a filer identifier is not passed in then the results will include filings submitted by any user in the firm.

                                      The intent for this call is to retrieve a subset of filings, not a complete historical record of all filings for the specified criteria; therefore the EFM imposes an upper bound of 1000 results. The most recent filings by filed date are returned. Selection and results list sort by descending date filed (reverse chronological order).

                                      Version2022.0
                                      RequiredCore functionality
                                      Accessible ToAny registered user. If CSM is enabled, requires the FilingHistory resource.
                                      User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)
                                      ServiceFilingReviewMDEService
                                      Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/v5/filingreviewservice.svc
                                      Request Message Definitionfilinglistrequest
                                      Response Message Definitionfilinglistresponse
                                      XML Samples
                                      DescriptionRequestResponse
                                      GetFilingListtyler-filinglistrequesttyler-filinglistresponse
                                      Inputs
                                      FieldDescription
                                      Court Location If populated, results will only include filings for the specified court location. If not populated, results will include filings for all court locations
                                      /filinglistrequest:GetFilingListRequestMessage/j:CaseCourt/nc:OrganizationIdentification/nc:IdentificationID
                                      Filing Status If populated, results will only include filings in the specified status.
                                      /filinglistrequest:GetFilingListRequestMessage/filinglistrequest:FilingListQueryCriteria/tylercommon:FilingListQueryCriteriaAugmentation/ecf:FilingStatus/ecf:FilingReviewStatusCode
                                      Case Number If populated, results will only include filings that match the case number
                                      /filinglistrequest:GetFilingListRequestMessage/filinglistrequest:FilingListQueryCriteria/j:CaseNumberText
                                      Date Range If StartDate and EndDate are populated, results will only include filings created within the designated date range
                                      /filinglistrequest:GetFilingListRequestMessage/filinglistrequest:FilingListQueryCriteria/nc:DateRange/nc:StartDate/nc:Date
                                      /filinglistrequest:GetFilingListRequestMessage/filinglistrequest:FilingListQueryCriteria/nc:DateRange/nc:EndDate/nc:Date
                                      Envelope Number If populated, results will only include filings that match the envelope number
                                      /filinglistrequest:GetFilingListRequestMessage/filinglistrequest:FilingListQueryCriteria/nc:DocumentIdentification/nc:IdentificationID
                                      Submitter If populated with an EFM UserId (obtained from GetUserList) results will only include filings for the specified user. If not populated, results will include filings for any users in the firm
                                      /filinglistrequest:GetFilingListRequestMessage/filinglistrequest:FilingListQueryCriteria/nc:DocumentSubmitter/nc:EntityPerson/nc:PersonOtherIdentification/nc:IdentificationID

                                      GetFilingStatus

                                      GetFilingStatus retrieves the status of a filing.

                                      NOTE: This API should not be used as an automated polling mechanism in lieu of implementing NotifyFilingReviewComplete

                                      Version2022.0
                                      RequiredCore functionality
                                      Accessible ToAny registered user. If CSM is enabled, requires the FilingHistory resource.
                                      User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)
                                      ServiceFilingReviewMDEService
                                      Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/v5/filingreviewservice.svc
                                      Request Message Definitionfilingstatusrequest
                                      Response Message Definitionfilingstatusresponse
                                      XML Samples
                                      DescriptionRequestResponse
                                      GetFilingStatustyler-filingstatusrequesttyler-filingstatusresponse
                                      GetFilingStatus - Detailstyler-detail-filingstatusrequesttyler-detail-filingstatusresponse
                                      GetFilingStatus - Acceptedtyler-detail-filingstatusrequesttyler-detail-filingstatusresponse-accepted
                                      GetFilingStatus - Rejectedtyler-detail-filingstatusrequesttyler-detail-filingstatusresponse-rejected
                                      Inputs
                                      FieldDescription
                                      Court Location The Court Locations code for this document Must be a valid court location identifier; however, the actual value provided does not affect the results of the API
                                      /filingstatusrequest:GetFilingStatusRequestMessage/j:CaseCourt/nc:OrganizationIdentification/nc:IdentificationID
                                      Filing ID The EFM's unique identifier for the desired filing
                                      /filingstatusrequest:GetFilingStatusRequestMessage/filingstatusrequest:FilingStatusQueryCriteria/nc:DocumentIdentification/nc:IdentificationID
                                      Include Details Boolean to request addtional details
                                      /filingstatusrequest:GetFilingStatusRequestMessage/tylercommon:GetFilingStatusRequestMessageAugmentation/tylercommon:IncludeFilingDetailIndicator

                                      PartialWaiver Provides details in regard to a standing waiver, if the filer has an active waiver on the case
                                      • ParentEnvelopeID - Identifies the envelope whereby the filer requested the waiver. Present only on filings that were submitted while the filer had an active waiver on the case
                                      • Outstanding balance - any remaining balance due from a filing whereby a standing waiver was requested
                                      • Court decision - GRANT if a waiver is granted either in part or in full, otherwise an empty value if the court has not yet decided
                                      • Percentage granted
                                      • URL of the court's payment system
                                      • Start and end date for the granted waiver

                                      Filing Assembly MDE Service

                                      The Filing Assembly MDE contains APIs whereby the EFM can call back into the EFSP in order to provide notification of events that have occurred within the EFM.
                                        • NotifyFilingReviewComplete
                                        • NotifyCourtDate
                                        The EFM does not sign the SOAP headers for callbacks to the EFSP. Details regarding the Filing Assembly MDE APIs are provided below.

                                        NotifyFilingReviewComplete

                                        The EFM calls NotifyFilingReviewComplete to notify the EFSP when a filing has been either accepted or rejected, unless the envelope was part of a batch (see NotifyBatchComplete for more information). Although an EFSP may submit multiple filings to the EFM within a single envelope via the ReviewFiling API, the EFM will call the EFSP once for each filing. However, these calls will not take place until the clerk has either accepted or rejected all of the filings in the envelope. The NotifyFilingReviewComplete request includes a compound message that consists of a ReviewFilingCallbackMessage and a PaymentReceiptMessage.


                                        In addition, the EFM will call NotifyFilingReviewComplete to notify the EFSP when the court renders a decision regarding a proposed order. In this scenario, the message will pertain to the child filing as depicted in the following diagram (click to enlarge).

                                        Version2022.0
                                        RequiredCore functionality
                                        Accessible ToEFM initiates this call therefore no user context
                                        ServiceFilingAssemblyMDEService

                                        Request Message Definitionreviewfilingcallback
                                        payment

                                        NotifyCourtDate

                                        NOTE: This API is currently restricted for use solely within the eFileIL market.
                                        NotifyCourtDate notifies the FilingAssembly MDE that a hearing has been scheduled. This API is applicable in two scenarios:
                                        • if the CMS automatically scheduled a hearing as a result of a filing
                                        • if the filer requested a hearing, which can only occur for court locations that have AllowHearing = True.
                                        Version2022.0
                                        RequiredConditional functionality, subject to business requirements
                                        Accessible ToEFM initiates this call therefore no user context

                                        /datecallback:NotifyCourtDateMessage/j:CaseCourt/nc:OrganizationIdentification/nc:IdentificationID
                                        Hearing Date/Time The start and end time of the hearing
                                        /datecallback:NotifyCourtDateMessage/nc:Case/j:CaseAugmentation/j:CaseCourtEvent/tylercommon:CourtEventAugmentation/tylercommon:CourtSchedule/tylercommon:ScheduleDayStartTime/nc:DateTime
                                        /datecallback:NotifyCourtDateMessage/nc:Case/j:CaseAugmentation/j:CaseCourtEvent/tylercommon:CourtEventAugmentation/tylercommon:CourtSchedule/tylercommon:ScheduleDayEndTime/nc:DateTime
                                        Courtroom The courtroom where the hearing will be held

                                        Court Record MDE Service

                                        The Court Record MDE enables an EFSP to query the EFM for information pertaining to existing cases. If the jurisdiction's Case Management System is integrated with the EFM, the EFM will request case information from the Case Management System. Otherwise, the EFM will provide the information it has about the case. Service information is maintained solely with the EFM, not the Case Management System.
                                          • GetCaseList
                                          • GetCase
                                          • GetDocument
                                          • GetServiceInformation
                                          The EFM does not support the ECF GetDocument API. Details regarding the Court Record MDE APIs are provided below.

                                          GetCaseList

                                          GetCaseList queries for a list of cases within a particular jurisdiction, matching on either the case number or a case participant's name. A search by case participant name is a search for an individual or an organization, not an individual within an organization. If the clerk's Case Management System is integrated with the EFM, this query will be forwarded to the CMS, otherwise the EFM will perform the query locally against its own indexes of known cases.

                                          The intent for this call is to retrieve a subset of cases, not a complete historical record of all cases for the specified criteria. Therefore, the EFM imposes an upper limit of 1000 results, where the returns are the most recent cases by date filed. The sort order of the selection and results are by descending date filed (reverse chronological) order.

                                          The case information may be dependent upon an integration to a clerk CMS. When an integration does not exist, the EFM will provide information about the cases that have been e-filed thus far. When an integration exists but is temporarily unavailable, the EFM will provide the most recent information it has

                                          GetCase

                                          GetCase queries for a case by the EFM's case identifier, which the EFSP obtains from the GetCaseList API. An EFSP must not cache case data; rather, the EFSP should always invoke the GetCase API to retrieve the latest information about the case.

                                          The case information may be dependent upon an integration to a clerk CMS. When an integration does not exist, the EFM will provide information about the cases that have been e-filed thus far. When an integration exists but is temporarily unavailable, the EFM will provide the most recent information it has

                                          Service MDE Service

                                          The Service MDE Service contains a single API for the purpose of initiating e-service without submitting a filing to the court.
                                            • ServeFiling
                                            • ServeProcess
                                            Details of the Service MDE Service API are provided below.

                                            ServeFiling

                                            ServeFiling submits a request for the EFM to perform electronic service only. The filing will not be submitted to the court.

                                            The request message is a FilingMessage. Please refer to ReviewFiling for more details about the FilingMessage. Since ECF does not define a Payment message for use with ServeFiling, any EFSP fees would be passed in via Tyler extensions within the CaseAugmentation element.

                                            The EFM asychronously invokes the NotifyFilingReviewComplete API for each filing as a callback to the EFSP to communicate the outcome of each filing.

                                            ServeFiling is not supported for:

                                            • non-indexed cases
                                            • filings that add a new party
                                            Version2022.0
                                            RequiredCore functionality
                                            Accessible ToAny registered user. If CSM is enabled, requires the SubmitEnvelopes resource.
                                            User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)
                                            ServiceServiceMDEService
                                            Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/v5/service.svc
                                            Request Message Definitionfiling
                                            Response Message Definitioncbrn
                                            XML Samples
                                            DescriptionRequestResponse
                                            ServeFilingtyler-servefilingrequesttyler-servefiling-response
                                            Inputs
                                            FieldDescription
                                            *** Refer to the Filing Message portion of the ReviewFiling API ***
                                            Charge Fees An indicator that the EFSP is charging fees for service.
                                            /payment:PaymentMessage/cac:AllowanceCharge/cbc:ChargeIndicator
                                            Fee Amount The EFSP fee amount to charge for service
                                            /payment:PaymentMessage/cac:AllowanceCharge/cbc:Amount
                                            Tax Percentage The percentage used to calculate the tax due
                                            /payment:PaymentMessage/cac:AllowanceCharge/cac:TaxCategory/cbc:Percent
                                            Tax Amount The amount of tax to collect for the EFSP fee
                                            /payment:PaymentMessage/cac:AllowanceCharge/cac:TaxTotal/cbc:TaxAmount
                                            Payment Account ID The EFM identifier for the payment account to charge
                                            /payment:PaymentMessage/cac:AllowanceCharge/cac:PaymentMeans/cbc:PaymentID
                                            Outputs
                                            FieldDescription
                                            Envelope Number IdentificationID provides the envelope number when IdentificationCategoryDescriptionText=envelopeID
                                            /cbrn:MessageStatus/ecf:MessageStatusAugmentation/nc:DocumentIdentification/nc:IdentificationID
                                            /cbrn:MessageStatus/ecf:MessageStatusAugmentation/nc:DocumentIdentification/nc:IdentificationCategoryDescriptionText



                                            ServeProcess

                                            ServeProcess is not supported.


                                            Court Scheduling MDE Service

                                            The Court Scheduling MDE contains APIs for the purpose of scheduling activities with the court.
                                              • GetCourtSchedule
                                              • RequestCourtDate
                                              • ReserveCourtDate
                                              Details of the Court Scheduling MDE APIs are provided below.

                                              GetCourtSchedule

                                              GetCourtSchedule is not currently supported by the EFM.


                                              RequestCourtDate

                                              NOTE: This API is currently restricted for use solely within the eFileIL market.
                                              RequestCourtDate requests available hearing dates for a case. One hearing date is allowed per envelope. This API is only available for court locations where AllowHearing = True. The hearing request must pertain to an existing envelope that has one or more filings in any of the following states:
                                              • Submitting
                                              • Submitted

                                              Furthermore, the user requesting the hearing must belong to envelope submitter's firm.

                                              ReserveCourtDate

                                              NOTE: This API is currently restricted for use solely within the eFileIL market.
                                              ReserveCourtDate requests a hearing date for a case. This API is only called if the EFM is configured to do so for the court location. One hearing date is allowed per envelope. This API is only available for court locations where AllowHearing = True. The hearing request must pertain to an existing envelope that has one or more filings in any of the following states:
                                              • Submitting
                                              • Submitted
                                              • Under Review
                                              Furthermore, the user requesting the hearing must belong to envelope submitter's firm. The message flow is depicted in the following diagram (click to enlarge).

                                              Version2022.0
                                              RequiredConditional functionality, subject to business requirements
                                              Accessible ToAny registered user. If CSM is enabled, requires the ScheduleHearing resource.
                                              User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)
                                              ServiceCourtSchedulingMDEService
                                              Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/v5/courtschedulingservice.svc
                                              Request Message Definitionreservedate
                                              Response Message Definitioncbrn
                                              XML Samples
                                              DescriptionRequestResponse
                                              ReserveCourtDatetyler-reservedatetyler-messagestatus
                                              Inputs
                                              FieldDescription
                                              Envelope Number The envelope number of the envelope to which the hearing request pertains
                                              /reservedate:ReserveCourtDateMessage/nc:DocumentIdentification/nc:IdentificationID
                                              /reservedate:ReserveCourtDateMessage/nc:DocumentIdentification/nc:IdentificationCategoryDescriptionText
                                              Court Location The court location identifier for the case to which the hearing request pertains
                                              /reservedate:ReserveCourtDateMessage/nc:Case/j:CaseAugmentation/j:CaseCourt/nc:OrganizationIdentification/nc:IdentificationID
                                              Estimated Duration Indicates an estimated duration for the requested hearing
                                              /reservedate:ReserveCourtDateMessage/reservedate:EstimatedDuration
                                              Time Range The StartDate and EndDate reflect a time range for the requested hearing
                                              /reservedate:ReserveCourtDateMessage/reservedate:PotentialStartTimeRange/nc:StartDate/nc:DateTime
                                              /reservedate:ReserveCourtDateMessage/reservedate:PotentialStartTimeRange/nc:EndDate/nc:DateTime
                                              Outputs
                                              FieldDescription
                                              Error If a hearing is unable to be reserved, the EFM will relay any error code and error message from the CMS
                                              /cbrn:MessageStatus/cbrn:MessageHandlingError/cbrn:ErrorCodeText
                                              /cbrn:MessageStatus/cbrn:MessageStatusCode
                                              Hearing ID The unique number of the hearing
                                              /cbrn:MessageStatus/ecf:MessageStatusAugmentation/nc:DocumentIdentification/nc:IdentificationID
                                              /cbrn:MessageStatus/ecf:MessageStatusAugmentation/nc:DocumentIdentification/nc:IdentificationCategoryDescriptionText

                                                Tyler Extension: Filing Assembly MDE Service

                                                The Tyler Extension Filing Assembly MDE Service contains APIs that Tyler has added to provide additional capabilities beyond what is defined within the ECF MDE.
                                                  • NotifyBatchComplete
                                                  • NotifyServiceComplete
                                                  • NotifyEvent
                                                  Details of the Tyler Extension Filing Assembly MDE Service APIs are provided below.

                                                  NotifyBatchComplete

                                                  The EFM calls NotifyBatchComplete to notify the EFSP when a batch of filings has completed clerk review. The EFM will not call NotifyFilingReviewComplete for envelopes that belong to a batch.

                                                  This API only applies to batch filing (available in limited jurisdictions).

                                                  Version2022.0
                                                  RequiredConditional functionality, subject to business requirements
                                                  Accessible ToEFM initiates this call therefore no user context
                                                  ServiceTylerFilingAssemblyMDEService
                                                  Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/v5/tylerfilingassemblyservice.svc
                                                  Request Message Definitionbatchcallback
                                                  Response Message Definitioncbrn

                                                  NotifyServiceComplete

                                                  NotifyServiceComplete is an optional API that an EFSP can implement in order to receive notification when one of the EFSP's customers has been served. Tyler must enable this API on a per EFSP per site basis.

                                                  An EFSP customer is defined as any registered user who has submitted a filing through the EFSP. Since registered users are separate from service contacts, this capability depends upon the correlation of a registered user and a service contact record. The EFM establishes this correlation when the email address of a user account matches the email address of a service contact.

                                                  Version2022.0
                                                  RequiredConditional functionality, subject to business requirements
                                                  Accessible ToEFM initiates this call therefore no user context
                                                  ServiceTylerFilingAssemblyMDEService
                                                  Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/v5/tylerfilingassemblyservice.svc
                                                  Request Message DefinitionServiceCallback
                                                  Response Message Definitioncbrn
                                                  XML Samples

                                                  NotifyEvent

                                                  NotifyEvent is an optional API that an EFSP can implement in order to receive notification of specific events that occur within the EFM. Tyler must enable this API on a per EFSP per site basis.

                                                  The request message utilizes a variable number of EventVariable elements, each of which denote a key/value pair. The particular key/value pairs vary according to the context of the notification.

                                                  Version2022.0
                                                  RequiredCore functionality
                                                  Accessible ToEFM initiates this call therefore no user context
                                                  ServiceFilingAssemblyMDEService
                                                  Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/v5/filingassemblyservice.svc
                                                  Request Message Definitionnotifyevent
                                                  common
                                                  Response Message Definitioncbrn
                                                  XML Samples
                                                  DescriptionRequestResponse
                                                  NotifyEvent - User Activationnotifyeventrequest-useractivationtyler-messagestatus
                                                  NotifyEvent - Password Resetnotifyeventrequest-passwordresettyler-messagestatus
                                                  NotifyEvent - Service Contact Removalnotifyeventrequest-servicecontactremovaltyler-messagestatus
                                                  NotifyEvent - Service Undeliverablenotifyeventrequest-serviceundeliverabletyler-messagestatus
                                                  Inputs
                                                  FieldDescription
                                                  EventTypeCode A code that defines the context of the notification. See the information below for definitions for each notification type
                                                  /eventcallback:NotifyEventMessage/eventcallback:EventTypeCode
                                                  EventKey An event key applicable to the event type code that triggered the notification
                                                  /eventcallback:NotifyEventMessage/eventcallback:Event/eventcallback:EventVariable/eventcallback:EventKey
                                                  EventValue The value that corresponds to the event key
                                                  /eventcallback:NotifyEventMessage/eventcallback:Event/eventcallback:EventVariable/eventcallback:EventValue
                                                  EventTypeCode=UserActivation indicates that the EFM has sent a user activation email. The call will be sent to the EFSP thru which the user registration took place
                                                  EventKey EventValue
                                                  UserID The EFM's unique identifier for the user
                                                  Email The user's email address
                                                  ActivationLink The URL for activating the user account
                                                  EventTypeCode=PasswordReset indicates that the EFM has sent a password reset email The call will be sent to the EFSP thru which the password reset took place
                                                  EventKey EventValue
                                                  UserID The EFM's unique identifier for the user
                                                  Email The user's email address
                                                  PasswordResetLink The URL for activating the user account
                                                  EventTypeCode=ServiceContactRemoval indicates that a service contact has been detached from a case

                                                  NOTE: This notification is only sent when:

                                                  • SendServiceContactRemovedNotifications is visible for the case's court location
                                                  • The email address associated to the service contact is also associated to a user
                                                  • The user has submitted at least one filing via the EFSP
                                                  • The EFSP is configured within the EFM as having the ability to receive event notifications
                                                  EventKey EventValue
                                                  ServiceContactID The EFM's unique identifier for the service contact
                                                  Email The service contact's email address
                                                  CaseNumber The court case number from which the service contact was removed
                                                  CaseTrackingID The EFM's unique identifier for the case
                                                  RemovedOn The timestamp when the removal occurred
                                                  RemovedByName The name of the person who removed the service contact
                                                  RemovedByEmail The email of the person who removed the service contact
                                                  EventTypeCode=ServiceUndeliverable indicates that the EFM was unable to complete service. The call will be sent to the EFSP thru which the request for service was received
                                                  EventKey EventValue
                                                  ServiceContactID The EFM identifier for the service contact
                                                  Email The email address of the service contact
                                                  CaseNumber The court case number for the case
                                                  CaseTrackingID The EFM identifier for the case
                                                  FilingID The EFM identifier for the filing
                                                  Outputs
                                                  FieldDescription
                                                  No Outputs



                                                  Tyler Extension: Court Record MDE Service

                                                  The Tyler Extension Court Record MDE Service contains APIs that Tyler has added to provide additional capabilities beyond what is defined within the ECF MDE.
                                                    • GetServiceCaseList
                                                    • GetServiceInformationHistory
                                                    Details of the Tyler Extension Court Record MDE Service APIs are provided below.

                                                    GetServiceCaseList

                                                    GetServiceCaseList retrieves a list of cases to which a service contact has been attached.

                                                    User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)

                                                    Tyler Extension: Court Scheduling MDE Service

                                                    The Tyler Extension Court Scheduling MDE Service contains APIs that Tyler has added to provide additional capabilities beyond what is defined within the ECF MDE.
                                                      • GetReturnDate
                                                      Details of the Tyler Extension Court Scheduliing MDE Service APIs are provided below.

                                                      GetReturnDate

                                                      NOTE: This API is currently restricted for use solely within the eFileIL market.
                                                      GetReturnDate calculates the first applicable return date based upon statute and/or local court rules. The return date pertains to the envelope, not the individual filings in the envelope. This API is only available for court locations where AllowReturnDate = True
                                                      Version2022.0
                                                      RequiredConditional functionality, subject to business requirements
                                                      Accessible ToAny registered user. If CSM is enabled, requires the ScheduleHearing resource.
                                                      User CredentialsUserNameHeader required in SOAP header with UserName (email) & Password (hash)
                                                      ServiceCourtSchedulingMDEService
                                                      Sample URLhttps://court.tylertech.cloud/efm/v5/tylercourtschedulingservice.svc
                                                      Request Message Definitionreturndaterequest
                                                      Response Message Definitionreturndateresponse
                                                      XML Samples
                                                      DescriptionRequestResponse
                                                      GetReturnDate - Initial Filingtyler-returndaterequest-efsp-initialtyler-returndateresponse
                                                      GetReturnDate - Subsequent Filingtyler-returndaterequest-efsp-subsequenttyler-returndateresponse
                                                      Inputs
                                                      FieldDescription
                                                      Date/Time Envelope Submitted The date and time that the envelope was submitted
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/nc:DocumentFiledDate/nc:DateTime
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/nc:DocumentPostDate/nc:DateTime
                                                      Court Location The Court Location code for the case being filed or filed into
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/j:CaseCourt/nc:OrganizationIdentification/nc:IdentificationID
                                                      Filing Code The Filing code the filer intends to submit
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/nc:Case/j:CaseAugmentation/j:CaseCourtEvent/tylercommon:CourtEventAugmentation/tylercommon:FilingCode
                                                      Motion Code The Motion Type code filer intends to submit
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/nc:Case/j:CaseAugmentation/j:CaseCourtEvent/tylercommon:CourtEventAugmentation/tylercommon:MotionTypeCode
                                                      Attorney Repeat this element as necessary to reflect attorneys relevant to this filing. IdentificationID provides the EFM identifier for an attorney within the filer's firm. Refer to the Attorney Management APIs for more information.
                                                      CaseRepresentedParty associates the attorney to the party being represented and can be repeated if representing multiple parties.
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/nc:Case/j:CaseAugmentation/j:CaseOfficial/nc:RoleOfPerson/ecf:PersonAugmentation/ecf:ParticipantID/nc:IdentificationID
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/nc:Case/j:CaseAugmentation/j:CaseOfficial/ecf:CaseOfficialAugmentation/ecf:CaseRepresentedParty
                                                      Case Category The Case Category code of the case
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/nc:Case/ecf:CaseAugmentation/ecf:CaseCategoryCode
                                                      Case Party Repeat this element for each case party relevant to this filing. Include any new case parties as well as any existing party for which an attorney is being added.
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/nc:Case/ecf:CaseAugmentation/ecf:CaseParty
                                                      Person or Organization EntityPerson represents a case participant that is either an individual or an attorney. EntityOrganization represents a case participant that is an organization. The s:id attribute establishes an identifier whereby the case party can be referenced elsewhere within the message.
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/nc:Case/ecf:CaseAugmentation/ecf:CaseParty/nc:EntityPerson
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/nc:Case/ecf:CaseAugmentation/ecf:CaseParty/nc:EntityOrganization
                                                      Case Party Role A valid PartyType code to indicate the case party's role role within the case.
                                                      Self Represented A boolean to indicate whether this is a self-represented litigant
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/nc:Case/ecf:CaseAugmentation/ecf:CaseParty/nc:EntityPerson/ecf:PersonAugmentation/ecf:CasePartySelfRepresentationIndicator
                                                      Case ID The EFM's unique ID for the case. Only applicable for subsequent filings
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/nc:Case/ecf:CaseAugmentation/ecf:CaseTrackingID/nc:IdentificationID
                                                      Case Type The Case Type code of the case
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/nc:Case/ecf:CaseAugmentation/ecf:CaseTypeCode
                                                      Out of State Flag to represent whether the filing includes out of state service
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/nc:Case/tylercommon:SchedulingAugmentation/tylercommon:OutOfStateIndicator
                                                      Return Date The requested return date for the envelope's filings
                                                      /returndate:ReturnDateMessage/nc:Case/tylercommon:SchedulingAugmentation/tylercommon:ReturnDate/nc:Date
                                                      Filing Party Reference to the filing party
